padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-63" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">0.5</span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-64" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">&nbsp;</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-65" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">M</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.969em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.497em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.652em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>1000</mn><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">W</mi></mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">M</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>1000</mn><mo>×</mo><mn>5.0</mn></mrow><mrow><mn>40</mn><mo>×</mo><mn>250</mn></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>0.5</mn><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">M</mi></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-6">\rm S=\frac{1000\ W}{MV}=\frac{1000\times5.0}{40\times250}=0.5\ M </script></span><br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৪২৪]</p>
</span>

                                            <p>দুর্বল এসিড ও সবল ক্ষারের বিক্রিয়ায় প্রশমন বিন্দুতে pH কত?</p>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: বিভিন্ন প্রশমন বিক্রিয়ায়,<br>
সবল এসিড ও সবল ক্ষারের প্রশমন বিন্দুতে pH&nbsp;= 7&nbsp;<br>
সবল এসিড ও দুর্বল ক্ষারের প্রশমন বিন্দুতে pH&nbsp;= 5.27&nbsp;<br>
দুর্বল এসিড ও সবল ক্ষারের প্রশমন বিন্দুতে pH&nbsp;= 8.80&nbsp;<br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৪৩৯]</p>

                                            <p>দুর্বল এসিড-দুর্বল ক্ষার টাইট্রেশনে উপযুক্ত নির্দেশক কোনটি?</p>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p><u>এসিড ও ক্ষারের প্রকৃতি</u>&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;<u>উপযুক্ত নির্দেশক</u><br>
সবল এসিড- সবল ক্ষার&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;সব নির্দেশক<br>
দুর্বল এসিড- সবল ক্ষার&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;ফেনলফ্‌থ্যালিন/থাইমল ব্লু (ক্ষার)<br>
সবল এসিড- দুর্বল ক্ষার&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;মিথাইল অরেঞ্জ/মিথাইল রেড<br>
দুর্বল এসিড- দুর্বল ক্ষার&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;কোনো নির্দেশকই উপযোগী নয়<br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৪৪০]</p>

                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>অক্সিজেনের ক্ষেত্রে সব সাধারণ অক্সাইডে (F বাদে) <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; margin-left: 0.125em;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.568em, 1000.9em, 4.264em, -999.998em); top: -4.506em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.449em;"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-710"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.568em, 1000.58em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-711" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">m</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.891em; left: 0.576em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-712" style="font-size: 50%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.404em, 1001.56em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -3.645em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.818em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-713" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">294.2</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.904em, 1001.72em, 1.191em, -999.998em); top: -1.268em; left: 0em;"><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: 0em; border-top: 1.5px solid; width: 1.723em; height: 0px;"></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.068em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-714" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">×</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-715" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">6</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.199em, 1006.15em, 4.305em, -999.998em); top: -0.736em; left: 0em;"><span class="mspace" id="MathJax-Span-716" style="height: 0em; vertical-align: 0em; width: 0em; display: inline-block; overflow: hidden;"></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-717" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">⇒</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-718" style="padding-left: 0.289em;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.273em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1000.82em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-719" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">m</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.85em; left: 0.822em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-720" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-721" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-722" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">1.614</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 5.207em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -4.197em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 5.252em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mfrac><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">e</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">e</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mfrac><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mfrac><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">M</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mfrac><mo>×</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">e</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">M</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mfrac><mo>×</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">e</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mfrac><mn>5</mn><mn>151.85</mn></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mn>294.2</mn></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mn>6</mn><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>1.614</mn></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-53">\rm \frac{n_1}{e_1}=\frac{n_2}{e_2}\Rightarrow\frac{m_1}{M_1}\times e_2=\frac{m_2}{M_2}\times e_1 \\
\Rightarrow\frac{5}{151.85}\times1=\frac{m_2}{294.2}\times6 \\
\Rightarrow m_2=1.614 </script></span><br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৪৬৮]</p>
</span>

                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>মিঠা পানির সর্বাপেক্ষা বৃহৎ উৎস কোনটি?</p>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>মিঠা পানির শতকরা পরিমাণ:<br>
(i) হিমবাহ ও তুষার আচ্ছাদন = 74%<br>
(ii) ভূ-গর্ভস্থ পানি = 22.2%&nbsp;<br>
(ii)&nbsp;বিভিন্ন হ্রদ = 0.3%<br>
(iv) বায়ুতে যা বৃষ্টিরূপে আসে = 0.035%<br>
(v) বিভিন্ন নদী = 0.03%<br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ১১০]</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>একটি <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-137-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>C</mi><msub><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>O</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1704" style="width: 1.928em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.559em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.15em, 1001.56em, 2.256em, -999.998em); top: -1.965em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1705"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1706" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">C</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1707"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.191em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.199em, 1000.74em, 4.182em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1708" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">O</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.85em; left: 0.781em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1709" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.969em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.247em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.153em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">O</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-137">\rm CO_2</script></span> অণুতে তিনটি পরমাণু থাকে।<br>
<span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-138-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo>&amp;#x2234;</mo></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1710" style="width: 0.658em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.535em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.6em, 1000.49em, 2.379em, -999.998em);
